    33	var (
    34	        keyMatch2Re = regexp.MustCompile(`:[^/]+`)
    35	        keyMatch3Re = regexp.MustCompile(`\{[^/]+\}`)
    36	        keyMatch4Re = regexp.MustCompile(`{([^/]+)}`)
    37	        keyMatch5Re = regexp.MustCompile(`\{[^/]+\}`)
    38	        keyGet2Re1  = regexp.MustCompile(`:[^/]+`)
    39	        keyGet3Re1  = regexp.MustCompile(`\{[^/]+?\}`) // non-greedy match of `{...}` to support multiple {} in `/.../`
    40	        reCache     = map[string]*regexp.Regexp{}
    41	        reCacheMu   = sync.RWMutex{}
    42	)
    43	
    44	func mustCompileOrGet(key string) *regexp.Regexp {
    45	        reCacheMu.RLock()
    46	        re, ok := reCache[key]
    47	        reCacheMu.RUnlock()
    48	
    49	        if !ok {
    50	                re = regexp.MustCompile(key)
    51	                reCacheMu.Lock()
    52	                reCache[key] = re
    53	                reCacheMu.Unlock()
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        return re
    57	}

    59	// validate the variadic parameter size and type as string.
    60	func validateVariadicArgs(expectedLen int, args ...interface{}) error {
    61	        if len(args) != expectedLen {
    62	                return fmt.Errorf("expected %d arguments, but got %d", expectedLen, len(args))
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        for _, p := range args {
    66	                _, ok := p.(string)
    67	                if !ok {
    68	                        return errors.New("argument must be a string")
    69	                }
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        return nil
    73	}

    76	func validateVariadicStringArgs(expectedLen int, args ...string) error {
    77	        if len(args) != expectedLen {
    78	                return fmt.Errorf("expected %d arguments, but got %d", expectedLen, len(args))
    79	        }
    80	        return nil

    83	// KeyMatch determines whether key1 matches the pattern of key2 (similar to RESTful path), key2 can contain a *.
    84	// For example, "/foo/bar" matches "/foo/*".
    85	func KeyMatch(key1 string, key2 string) bool {
    86	        i := strings.Index(key2, "*")
    87	        if i == -1 {
    88	                return key1 == key2
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        if len(key1) > i {
    92	                return key1[:i] == key2[:i]
    93	        }
    94	        return key1 == key2[:i]
    95	}
    96	
    97	// KeyMatchFunc is the wrapper for KeyMatch.
    98	func KeyMatchFunc(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
    99	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   100	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyMatch", err)
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   104	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   105	
   106	        return KeyMatch(name1, name2), nil
   107	}
   108	
   109	// KeyGet returns the matched part
   110	// For example, "/foo/bar/foo" matches "/foo/*"
   111	// "bar/foo" will been returned.
   112	func KeyGet(key1, key2 string) string {
   113	        i := strings.Index(key2, "*")
   114	        if i == -1 {
   115	                return ""
   116	        }
   117	        if len(key1) > i {
   118	                if key1[:i] == key2[:i] {
   119	                        return key1[i:]
   120	                }
   121	        }
   122	        return ""
   123	}
   124	
   125	// KeyGetFunc is the wrapper for KeyGet.
   126	func KeyGetFunc(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   127	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   128	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyGet", err)
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   132	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   133	
   134	        return KeyGet(name1, name2), nil
   135	}

   137	// KeyMatch2 determines whether key1 matches the pattern of key2 (similar to RESTful path), key2 can contain a *.
   138	// For example, "/foo/bar" matches "/foo/*", "/resource1" matches "/:resource".
   139	func KeyMatch2(key1 string, key2 string) bool {
   140	        key2 = strings.Replace(key2, "/*", "/.*", -1)
   141	
   142	        key2 = keyMatch2Re.ReplaceAllString(key2, "$1[^/]+$2")
   143	
   144	        return RegexMatch(key1, "^"+key2+"$")
   145	}
   146	
   147	// KeyMatch2Func is the wrapper for KeyMatch2.
   148	func KeyMatch2Func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   149	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   150	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyMatch2", err)
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   154	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   155	
   156	        return KeyMatch2(name1, name2), nil
   157	}
   158	
   159	// KeyGet2 returns value matched pattern
   160	// For example, "/resource1" matches "/:resource"
   161	// if the pathVar == "resource", then "resource1" will be returned.
   162	func KeyGet2(key1, key2 string, pathVar string) string {
   163	        key2 = strings.Replace(key2, "/*", "/.*", -1)
   164	        keys := keyGet2Re1.FindAllString(key2, -1)
   165	        key2 = keyGet2Re1.ReplaceAllString(key2, "$1([^/]+)$2")
   166	        key2 = "^" + key2 + "$"
   167	
   168	        re := mustCompileOrGet(key2)
   169	        values := re.FindAllStringSubmatch(key1, -1)
   170	        if len(values) == 0 {
   171	                return ""
   172	        }
   173	        for i, key := range keys {
   174	                if pathVar == key[1:] {
   175	                        return values[0][i+1]
   176	                }
   177	        }
   178	        return ""
   179	}
   180	
   181	// KeyGet2Func is the wrapper for KeyGet2.
   182	func KeyGet2Func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   183	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(3, args...); err != nil {
   184	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyGet2", err)
   185	        }
   186	
   187	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   188	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   189	        key := args[2].(string)
   190	
   191	        return KeyGet2(name1, name2, key), nil
   192	}
   193	
   194	// KeyMatch3 determines whether key1 matches the pattern of key2 (similar to RESTful path), key2 can contain a *.
   195	// For example, "/foo/bar" matches "/foo/*", "/resource1" matches "/{resource}".
   196	func KeyMatch3(key1 string, key2 string) bool {
   197	        key2 = strings.Replace(key2, "/*", "/.*", -1)
   198	        key2 = keyMatch3Re.ReplaceAllString(key2, "$1[^/]+$2")
   199	
   200	        return RegexMatch(key1, "^"+key2+"$")
   201	}
   202	
   203	// KeyMatch3Func is the wrapper for KeyMatch3.
   204	func KeyMatch3Func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   205	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   206	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyMatch3", err)
   207	        }
   208	
   209	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   210	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   211	
   212	        return KeyMatch3(name1, name2), nil
   213	}
   214	
   215	// KeyGet3 returns value matched pattern
   216	// For example, "project/proj_project1_admin/" matches "project/proj_{project}_admin/"
   217	// if the pathVar == "project", then "project1" will be returned.
   218	func KeyGet3(key1, key2 string, pathVar string) string {
   219	        key2 = strings.Replace(key2, "/*", "/.*", -1)
   220	
   221	        keys := keyGet3Re1.FindAllString(key2, -1)
   222	        key2 = keyGet3Re1.ReplaceAllString(key2, "$1([^/]+?)$2")
   223	        key2 = "^" + key2 + "$"
   224	        re := mustCompileOrGet(key2)
   225	        values := re.FindAllStringSubmatch(key1, -1)
   226	        if len(values) == 0 {
   227	                return ""
   228	        }
   229	        for i, key := range keys {
   230	                if pathVar == key[1:len(key)-1] {
   231	                        return values[0][i+1]
   232	                }
   233	        }
   234	        return ""
   235	}
   236	
   237	// KeyGet3Func is the wrapper for KeyGet3.
   238	func KeyGet3Func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   239	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(3, args...); err != nil {
   240	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyGet3", err)
   241	        }
   242	
   243	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   244	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   245	        key := args[2].(string)
   246	
   247	        return KeyGet3(name1, name2, key), nil
   248	}
   249	
   250	// KeyMatch4 determines whether key1 matches the pattern of key2 (similar to RESTful path), key2 can contain a *.
   251	// Besides what KeyMatch3 does, KeyMatch4 can also match repeated patterns:
   252	// "/parent/123/child/123" matches "/parent/{id}/child/{id}"
   253	// "/parent/123/child/456" does not match "/parent/{id}/child/{id}"
   254	// But KeyMatch3 will match both.
   255	func KeyMatch4(key1 string, key2 string) bool {
   256	        key2 = strings.Replace(key2, "/*", "/.*", -1)
   257	
   258	        tokens := []string{}
   259	
   260	        re := keyMatch4Re
   261	        key2 = re.ReplaceAllStringFunc(key2, func(s string) string {
   262	                tokens = append(tokens, s[1:len(s)-1])
   263	                return "([^/]+)"
   264	        })
   265	
   266	        re = mustCompileOrGet("^" + key2 + "$")
   267	        matches := re.FindStringSubmatch(key1)
   268	        if matches == nil {
   269	                return false
   270	        }
   271	        matches = matches[1:]
   272	
   273	        if len(tokens) != len(matches) {
   274	                panic(errors.New("KeyMatch4: number of tokens is not equal to number of values"))
   275	        }
   276	
   277	        values := map[string]string{}
   278	
   279	        for key, token := range tokens {
   280	                if _, ok := values[token]; !ok {
   281	                        values[token] = matches[key]
   282	                }
   283	                if values[token] != matches[key] {
   284	                        return false
   285	                }
   286	        }
   287	
   288	        return true
   289	}
   290	
   291	// KeyMatch4Func is the wrapper for KeyMatch4.
   292	func KeyMatch4Func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   293	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   294	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyMatch4", err)
   295	        }
   296	
   297	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   298	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   299	
   300	        return KeyMatch4(name1, name2), nil
   301	}
   302	
   303	// KeyMatch5 determines whether key1 matches the pattern of key2 (similar to RESTful path), key2 can contain a *
   304	// For example,
   305	// - "/foo/bar?status=1&type=2" matches "/foo/bar"
   306	// - "/parent/child1" and "/parent/child1" matches "/parent/*"
   307	// - "/parent/child1?status=1" matches "/parent/*".
   308	func KeyMatch5(key1 string, key2 string) bool {
   309	        i := strings.Index(key1, "?")
   310	
   311	        if i != -1 {
   312	                key1 = key1[:i]
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        key2 = strings.Replace(key2, "/*", "/.*", -1)
   316	        key2 = keyMatch5Re.ReplaceAllString(key2, "$1[^/]+$2")
   317	
   318	        return RegexMatch(key1, "^"+key2+"$")
   319	}
   320	
   321	// KeyMatch5Func is the wrapper for KeyMatch5.
   322	func KeyMatch5Func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   323	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   324	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "keyMatch5", err)
   325	        }
   326	
   327	        name1 := args[0].(string)
   328	        name2 := args[1].(string)
   329	
   330	        return KeyMatch5(name1, name2), nil
   331	}

   333	// RegexMatch determines whether key1 matches the pattern of key2 in regular expression.
   334	func RegexMatch(key1 string, key2 string) bool {
   335	        res, err := regexp.MatchString(key2, key1)
   336	        if err != nil {
   337	                panic(err)
   338	        }
   339	        return res
   340	}

   354	// IPMatch determines whether IP address ip1 matches the pattern of IP address ip2, ip2 can be an IP address or a CIDR pattern.
   355	// For example, "192.168.2.123" matches "192.168.2.0/24".
   356	func IPMatch(ip1 string, ip2 string) bool {
   357	        objIP1 := net.ParseIP(ip1)
   358	        if objIP1 == nil {
   359	                panic("invalid argument: ip1 in IPMatch() function is not an IP address.")
   360	        }
   361	
   362	        _, cidr, err := net.ParseCIDR(ip2)
   363	        if err != nil {
   364	                objIP2 := net.ParseIP(ip2)
   365	                if objIP2 == nil {
   366	                        panic("invalid argument: ip2 in IPMatch() function is neither an IP address nor a CIDR.")
   367	                }
   368	
   369	                return objIP1.Equal(objIP2)
   370	        }
   371	
   372	        return cidr.Contains(objIP1)
   373	}
   374	
   375	// IPMatchFunc is the wrapper for IPMatch.
   376	func IPMatchFunc(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   377	        if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   378	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "ipMatch", err)
   379	        }
   380	
   381	        ip1 := args[0].(string)
   382	        ip2 := args[1].(string)
   383	
   384	        return IPMatch(ip1, ip2), nil
   385	}

   404	// GenerateGFunction is the factory method of the g(_, _[, _]) function.
   405	func GenerateGFunction(rm rbac.RoleManager) govaluate.ExpressionFunction {
   406	        memorized := sync.Map{}
   407	        return func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   408	                // Like all our other govaluate functions, all args are strings.
   409	
   410	                // Allocate and generate a cache key from the arguments...
   411	                total := len(args)
   412	                for _, a := range args {
   413	                        aStr := a.(string)
   414	                        total += len(aStr)
   415	                }
   416	                builder := strings.Builder{}
   417	                builder.Grow(total)
   418	                for _, arg := range args {
   419	                        builder.WriteByte(0)
   420	                        builder.WriteString(arg.(string))
   421	                }
   422	                key := builder.String()
   423	
   424	                // ...and see if we've already calculated this.
   425	                v, found := memorized.Load(key)
   426	                if found {
   427	                        return v, nil
   428	                }
   429	
   430	                // If not, do the calculation.
   431	                // There are guaranteed to be exactly 2 or 3 arguments.
   432	                name1, name2 := args[0].(string), args[1].(string)
   433	                if rm == nil {
   434	                        v = name1 == name2
   435	                } else if len(args) == 2 {
   436	                        v, _ = rm.HasLink(name1, name2)
   437	                } else {
   438	                        domain := args[2].(string)
   439	                        v, _ = rm.HasLink(name1, name2, domain)
   440	                }
   441	
   442	                memorized.Store(key, v)
   443	                return v, nil
   444	        }
   445	}
   446	
   447	// GenerateConditionalGFunction is the factory method of the g(_, _[, _]) function with conditions.
   448	func GenerateConditionalGFunction(crm rbac.ConditionalRoleManager) govaluate.ExpressionFunction {
   449	        return func(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
   450	                // Like all our other govaluate functions, all args are strings.
   451	                var hasLink bool
   452	
   453	                name1, name2 := args[0].(string), args[1].(string)
   454	                if crm == nil {
   455	                        hasLink = name1 == name2
   456	                } else if len(args) == 2 {
   457	                        hasLink, _ = crm.HasLink(name1, name2)
   458	                } else {
   459	                        domain := args[2].(string)
   460	                        hasLink, _ = crm.HasLink(name1, name2, domain)
   461	                }
   462	
   463	                return hasLink, nil
   464	        }
   465	}
   466

   471	        if err := validateVariadicStringArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
   472	                return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "TimeMatch", err)
   473	        }
   474	        return TimeMatch(args[0], args[1])
   475	}
   476	
   477	// TimeMatch determines whether the current time is between startTime and endTime.
   478	// You can use "_" to indicate that the parameter is ignored.
   479	func TimeMatch(startTime, endTime string) (bool, error) {
   480	        now := time.Now()
   481	        if startTime != "_" {
   482	                if start, err := time.Parse("2006-01-02 15:04:05", startTime); err != nil {
   483	                        return false, err
   484	                } else if !now.After(start) {
   485	                        return false, nil
   486	                }
   487	        }
   488	
   489	        if endTime != "_" {
   490	                if end, err := time.Parse("2006-01-02 15:04:05", endTime); err != nil {
   491	                        return false, err
   492	                } else if !now.Before(end) {
   493	                        return false, nil
   494	                }
   495	        }
   496	
   497	        return true, nil
   498	}

    29	// [string]govaluate.ExpressionFunction
    30	
    31	// AddFunction adds an expression function.
    32	func (fm *FunctionMap) AddFunction(name string, function govaluate.ExpressionFunction) {
    33	        fm.fns.LoadOrStore(name, function)
    34	}
    35

    58	        ret := make(map[string]govaluate.ExpressionFunction)
    59

    25	var evalReg = regexp.MustCompile(`\beval\((?P<rule>[^)]*)\)`)

    27	var escapeAssertionRegex = regexp.MustCompile(`\b((r|p)[0-9]*)\.`)
    28	
    29	func JsonToMap(jsonStr string) (map[string]interface{}, error) {
    30	        result := make(map[string]interface{})
    31	        err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(jsonStr), &result)
    32	        if err != nil {
    33	                return result, err
    34	        }
    35	        return result, nil
    36	}

    38	// EscapeAssertion escapes the dots in the assertion, because the expression evaluation doesn't support such variable names.
    39	func EscapeAssertion(s string) string {
    40	        s = escapeAssertionRegex.ReplaceAllStringFunc(s, func(m string) string {
    41	                return strings.Replace(m, ".", "_", 1)
    42	        })
    43	        return s
    44	}
    45	
    46	// RemoveComments removes the comments starting with # in the text.
    47	func RemoveComments(s string) string {
    48	        pos := strings.Index(s, "#")
    49	        if pos == -1 {
    50	                return s
    51	        }
    52	        return strings.TrimSpace(s[0:pos])
    53	}

    55	// ArrayEquals determines whether two string arrays are identical.
    56	func ArrayEquals(a []string, b []string) bool {
    57	        if len(a) != len(b) {
    58	                return false
    59	        }
    60	
    61	        for i, v := range a {
    62	                if v != b[i] {
    63	                        return false
    64	                }
    65	        }
    66	        return true
    67	}
    68	
    69	// Array2DEquals determines whether two 2-dimensional string arrays are identical.
    70	func Array2DEquals(a [][]string, b [][]string) bool {
    71	        if len(a) != len(b) {
    72	                return false
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        for i, v := range a {
    76	                if !ArrayEquals(v, b[i]) {
    77	                        return false
    78	                }
    79	        }
    80	        return true
    81	}
    82	
    83	// SortArray2D  Sorts the two-dimensional string array.
    84	func SortArray2D(arr [][]string) {
    85	        if len(arr) == 0 {
    86	                return
    87	        }
    88	        sort.Slice(arr, func(i, j int) bool {
    89	                minArrLen := len(arr[i])
    90	                if len(arr[j]) < minArrLen {
    91	                        minArrLen = len(arr[j])
    92	                }
    93	                for k := 0; k < minArrLen; k++ {
    94	                        if arr[i][k] != arr[j][k] {
    95	                                return arr[i][k] < arr[j][k]
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                return len(arr[i]) < len(arr[j])
    99	        })
   100	}
   101	
   102	// SortedArray2DEquals determines whether two 2-dimensional string arrays are identical.
   103	func SortedArray2DEquals(a [][]string, b [][]string) bool {
   104	        if len(a) != len(b) {
   105	                return false
   106	        }
   107	        copyA := make([][]string, len(a))
   108	        copy(copyA, a)
   109	        copyB := make([][]string, len(b))
   110	        copy(copyB, b)
   111	
   112	        SortArray2D(copyA)
   113	        SortArray2D(copyB)
   114	
   115	        for i, v := range copyA {
   116	                if !ArrayEquals(v, copyB[i]) {
   117	                        return false
   118	                }
   119	        }
   120	        return true
   121	}
   122	
   123	// ArrayRemoveDuplicates removes any duplicated elements in a string array.
   124	func ArrayRemoveDuplicates(s *[]string) {
   125	        found := make(map[string]bool)
   126	        j := 0
   127	        for i, x := range *s {
   128	                if !found[x] {
   129	                        found[x] = true
   130	                        (*s)[j] = (*s)[i]
   131	                        j++
   132	                }
   133	        }
   134	        *s = (*s)[:j]
   135	}

   138	func ArrayToString(s []string) string {
   139	        return strings.Join(s, ", ")
   140	}
   141	
   142	// ParamsToString gets a printable string for variable number of parameters.
   143	func ParamsToString(s ...string) string {
   144	        return strings.Join(s, ", ")
   145	}

   147	// SetEquals determines whether two string sets are identical.
   148	func SetEquals(a []string, b []string) bool {
   149	        if len(a) != len(b) {
   150	                return false
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        sort.Strings(a)
   154	        sort.Strings(b)
   155	
   156	        for i, v := range a {
   157	                if v != b[i] {
   158	                        return false
   159	                }
   160	        }
   161	        return true
   162	}

   164	// SetEquals determines whether two int sets are identical.
   165	func SetEqualsInt(a []int, b []int) bool {
   166	        if len(a) != len(b) {
   167	                return false
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        sort.Ints(a)
   171	        sort.Ints(b)
   172	
   173	        for i, v := range a {
   174	                if v != b[i] {
   175	                        return false
   176	                }
   177	        }
   178	        return true
   179	}
   180	
   181	// Set2DEquals determines whether two string slice sets are identical.
   182	func Set2DEquals(a [][]string, b [][]string) bool {
   183	        if len(a) != len(b) {
   184	                return false
   185	        }
   186	
   187	        var aa []string
   188	        for _, v := range a {
   189	                sort.Strings(v)
   190	                aa = append(aa, strings.Join(v, ", "))
   191	        }
   192	        var bb []string
   193	        for _, v := range b {
   194	                sort.Strings(v)
   195	                bb = append(bb, strings.Join(v, ", "))
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        return SetEquals(aa, bb)
   199	}

   201	// JoinSlice joins a string and a slice into a new slice.
   202	func JoinSlice(a string, b ...string) []string {
   203	        res := make([]string, 0, len(b)+1)
   204	
   205	        res = append(res, a)
   206	        res = append(res, b...)
   207	
   208	        return res
   209	}
   210	
   211	// JoinSliceAny joins a string and a slice into a new interface{} slice.
   212	func JoinSliceAny(a string, b ...string) []interface{} {
   213	        res := make([]interface{}, 0, len(b)+1)
   214	
   215	        res = append(res, a)
   216	        for _, s := range b {
   217	                res = append(res, s)
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        return res
   221	}
   222	
   223	// SetSubtract returns the elements in `a` that aren't in `b`.
   224	func SetSubtract(a []string, b []string) []string {
   225	        mb := make(map[string]struct{}, len(b))
   226	        for _, x := range b {
   227	                mb[x] = struct{}{}
   228	        }
   229	        var diff []string
   230	        for _, x := range a {
   231	                if _, found := mb[x]; !found {
   232	                        diff = append(diff, x)
   233	                }
   234	        }
   235	        return diff
   236	}
   237	
   238	// HasEval determine whether matcher contains function eval.
   239	func HasEval(s string) bool {
   240	        return evalReg.MatchString(s)
   241	}
   242	
   243	// ReplaceEval replace function eval with the value of its parameters.
   244	func ReplaceEval(s string, rule string) string {
   245	        return evalReg.ReplaceAllString(s, "("+rule+")")
   246	}
   247	
   248	// ReplaceEvalWithMap replace function eval with the value of its parameters via given sets.
   249	func ReplaceEvalWithMap(src string, sets map[string]string) string {
   250	        return evalReg.ReplaceAllStringFunc(src, func(s string) string {
   251	                subs := evalReg.FindStringSubmatch(s)
   252	                if subs == nil {
   253	                        return s
   254	                }
   255	                key := subs[1]
   256	                value, found := sets[key]
   257	                if !found {
   258	                        return s
   259	                }
   260	                return evalReg.ReplaceAllString(s, value)
   261	        })
   262	}
   263	
   264	// GetEvalValue returns the parameters of function eval.
   265	func GetEvalValue(s string) []string {
   266	        subMatch := evalReg.FindAllStringSubmatch(s, -1)
   267	        var rules []string
   268	        for _, rule := range subMatch {
   269	                rules = append(rules, rule[1])
   270	        }
   271	        return rules
   272	}
   273	
   274	func RemoveDuplicateElement(s []string) []string {
   275	        result := make([]string, 0, len(s))
   276	        temp := map[string]struct{}{}
   277	        for _, item := range s {
   278	                if _, ok := temp[item]; !ok {
   279	                        temp[item] = struct{}{}
   280	                        result = append(result, item)
   281	                }
   282	        }
   283	        return result
   284	}
   285	
   286	type node struct {
   287	        key   interface{}
   288	        value interface{}
   289	        prev  *node
   290	        next  *node
   291	}
   292	
   293	type LRUCache struct {
   294	        capacity int
   295	        m        map[interface{}]*node
   296	        head     *node
   297	        tail     *node
   298	}
   299	
   300	func NewLRUCache(capacity int) *LRUCache {
   301	        cache := &LRUCache{}
   302	        cache.capacity = capacity
   303	        cache.m = map[interface{}]*node{}
   304	
   305	        head := &node{}
   306	        tail := &node{}
   307	
   308	        head.next = tail
   309	        tail.prev = head
   310	
   311	        cache.head = head
   312	        cache.tail = tail
   313	
   314	        return cache
   315	}
   316	
   317	func (cache *LRUCache) remove(n *node, listOnly bool) {
   318	        if !listOnly {
   319	                delete(cache.m, n.key)
   320	        }
   321	        n.prev.next = n.next
   322	        n.next.prev = n.prev
   323	}
   324	
   325	func (cache *LRUCache) add(n *node, listOnly bool) {
   326	        if !listOnly {
   327	                cache.m[n.key] = n
   328	        }
   329	        headNext := cache.head.next
   330	        cache.head.next = n
   331	        headNext.prev = n
   332	        n.next = headNext
   333	        n.prev = cache.head
   334	}
   335	
   336	func (cache *LRUCache) moveToHead(n *node) {
   337	        cache.remove(n, true)
   338	        cache.add(n, true)
   339	}
   340	
   341	func (cache *LRUCache) Get(key interface{}) (value interface{}, ok bool) {
   342	        n, ok := cache.m[key]
   343	        if ok {
   344	                cache.moveToHead(n)
   345	                return n.value, ok
   346	        } else {
   347	                return nil, ok
   348	        }
   349	}
   350	
   351	func (cache *LRUCache) Put(key interface{}, value interface{}) {
   352	        n, ok := cache.m[key]
   353	        if ok {
   354	                cache.remove(n, false)
   355	        } else {
   356	                n = &node{key, value, nil, nil}
   357	                if len(cache.m) >= cache.capacity {
   358	                        cache.remove(cache.tail.prev, false)
   359	                }
   360	        }
   361	        cache.add(n, false)
   362	}
   363	
   364	type SyncLRUCache struct {
   365	        rwm sync.RWMutex
   366	        *LRUCache
   367	}
   368	
   369	func NewSyncLRUCache(capacity int) *SyncLRUCache {
   370	        cache := &SyncLRUCache{}
   371	        cache.LRUCache = NewLRUCache(capacity)
   372	        return cache
   373	}
   374	
   375	func (cache *SyncLRUCache) Get(key interface{}) (value interface{}, ok bool) {
   376	        cache.rwm.Lock()
   377	        defer cache.rwm.Unlock()
   378	        return cache.LRUCache.Get(key)
   379	}
   380	
   381	func (cache *SyncLRUCache) Put(key interface{}, value interface{}) {
   382	        cache.rwm.Lock()
   383	        defer cache.rwm.Unlock()
   384	        cache.LRUCache.Put(key, value)
   385	}

   119	// GetFilteredNamedPolicyWithMatcher gets rules based on matcher from the policy.
   120	func (e *Enforcer) GetFilteredNamedPolicyWithMatcher(ptype string, matcher string) ([][]string, error) {
   121	        var res [][]string
   122	        var err error
   123	
   124	        functions := e.fm.GetFunctions()
   125	        if _, ok := e.model["g"]; ok {
   126	                for key, ast := range e.model["g"] {
   127	                        // g must be a normal role definition (ast.RM != nil)
   128	                        //   or a conditional role definition (ast.CondRM != nil)
   129	                        // ast.RM and ast.CondRM shouldn't be nil at the same time
   130	                        if ast.RM != nil {
   131	                                functions[key] = util.GenerateGFunction(ast.RM)
   132	                        }
   133	                        if ast.CondRM != nil {
   134	                                functions[key] = util.GenerateConditionalGFunction(ast.CondRM)
   135	                        }
   136	                }
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        var expString string
   140	        if matcher == "" {
   141	                return res, fmt.Errorf("matcher is empty")
   142	        } else {
   143	                expString = util.RemoveComments(util.EscapeAssertion(matcher))
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        var expression *govaluate.EvaluableExpression
   147	
   148	        expression, err = govaluate.NewEvaluableExpressionWithFunctions(expString, functions)
   149	        if err != nil {
   150	                return res, err
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        pTokens := make(map[string]int, len(e.model["p"][ptype].Tokens))
   154	        for i, token := range e.model["p"][ptype].Tokens {
   155	                pTokens[token] = i
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        parameters := enforceParameters{
   159	                pTokens: pTokens,
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        if policyLen := len(e.model["p"][ptype].Policy); policyLen != 0 && strings.Contains(expString, ptype+"_") {
   163	                for _, pvals := range e.model["p"][ptype].Policy {
   164	                        if len(e.model["p"][ptype].Tokens) != len(pvals) {
   165	                                return res, fmt.Errorf(
   166	                                        "invalid policy size: expected %d, got %d, pvals: %v",
   167	                                        len(e.model["p"][ptype].Tokens),
   168	                                        len(pvals),
   169	                                        pvals)
   170	                        }
   171	
   172	                        parameters.pVals = pvals
   173	
   174	                        result, err := expression.Eval(parameters)
   175	
   176	                        if err != nil {
   177	                                return res, err
   178	                        }
   179	
   180	                        switch result := result.(type) {
   181	                        case bool:
   182	                                if result {
   183	                                        res = append(res, pvals)
   184	                                }
   185	                        case float64:
   186	                                if result != 0 {
   187	                                        res = append(res, pvals)
   188	                                }
   189	                        default:
   190	                                return res, errors.New("matcher result should be bool, int or float")
   191	                        }
   192	                }
   193	        }
   194	        return res, nil
   195	}
   196

   202	// HasNamedPolicy determines whether a named authorization rule exists.
   203	func (e *Enforcer) HasNamedPolicy(ptype string, params ...interface{}) (bool, error) {
   204	        if strSlice, ok := params[0].([]string); len(params) == 1 && ok {
   205	                return e.model.HasPolicy("p", ptype, strSlice)
   206	        }
   207	
   208	        policy := make([]string, 0)
   209	        for _, param := range params {
   210	                policy = append(policy, param.(string))
   211	        }
   212	
   213	        return e.model.HasPolicy("p", ptype, policy)
   214	}

   174	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/foo", "/foo", true)
   175	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/foo", "/foo*", true)
   176	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/foo", "/foo/*", false)

   179	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/foo/bar", "/foo/*", true)
   180	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/foobar", "/foo", false)
   181	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/foobar", "/foo*", false)
   182	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/foobar", "/foo/*", false)
   183	
   184	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/", "/{resource}", false)
   185	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/resource1", "/{resource}", true)
   186	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/myid", "/{id}/using/{resId}", false)
   187	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/myid/using/myresid", "/{id}/using/{resId}", true)
   188	
   189	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/proxy/myid", "/proxy/{id}/*", false)
   190	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/proxy/myid/", "/proxy/{id}/*", true)
   191	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/proxy/myid/res", "/proxy/{id}/*", true)
   192	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/proxy/myid/res/res2", "/proxy/{id}/*", true)
   193	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/proxy/myid/res/res2/res3", "/proxy/{id}/*", true)
   194	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/proxy/", "/proxy/{id}/*", false)
   195	
   196	        testKeyMatch3(t, "/myid/using/myresid", "/{id/using/{resId}", false)
   197	}

        t.Helper()

                t.Errorf("Enforce Error: %s", err)
        } else if myRes != res {
                t.Errorf("%s, %v, %s: %t, supposed to be %t", sub, obj, act, myRes, res)

func testEnforce(t *testing.T, e *Enforcer, sub interface{}, obj interface{}, act string, res bool) {
        t.Helper()
        if myRes, err := e.Enforce(sub, obj, act); err != nil {
                t.Errorf("Enforce Error: %s", err)
        } else if myRes != res {
                t.Errorf("%s, %v, %s: %t, supposed to be %t", sub, obj, act, myRes, res)
func TestBLP(t *testing.T) {
e, _ := NewEnforcer("examples/blp_model.conf", "examples/blp_policy.csv")

// Test case for BLP model
// Alice has top secret security level, she can read data1 (top secret) and write data2 (secret) is not allowed?
// BLP: no read up, no write down.

// alice: 3 (top secret)
// bob: 2 (secret)
// data1: 3
// data2: 2

res, _ := e.Enforce("alice", "data1", "read") // 3 >= 3, ok
if res != true {
should be able to read data1")
}
res, _ = e.Enforce("alice", "data2", "read") // 3 >= 2, ok
if res != true {
should be able to read data2")
}
res, _ = e.Enforce("alice", "data1", "write") // 3 <= 3, ok
if res != true {
should be able to write data1")
}
res, _ = e.Enforce("alice", "data2", "write") // 3 <= 2, false
if res != false {
should not be able to write data2")
}

res, _ = e.Enforce("bob", "data1", "read") // 2 >= 3, false
if res != false {
should not be able to read data1")
}
}

        }
}

                t.Errorf("%s, %s: %t, supposed to be %t", obj, act, myRes, res)
        }
}

// GenerateGFunction is the factory method of the g(_, _[, _]) function.
func GenerateGFunction(rm rbac.RoleManager) govaluate.ExpressionFunction {

// BlpMatch determines whether level1 matches the level2 of BLP model.
func BlpMatch(level1 string, level2 string) bool {
return level1 >= level2
}

// BlpMatchFunc is the wrapper for BlpMatch.
func BlpMatchFunc(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
 false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "blpMatch", err)
}

level1 := args[0].(string)
level2 := args[1].(string)

return BlpMatch(level1, level2), nil
}

+// BlpMatch determines whether level1 matches the level2 of BLP model.
+func BlpMatch(level1 string, level2 string) bool {
+	return level1 >= level2
+}
+
+// BlpMatchFunc is the wrapper for BlpMatch.
+func BlpMatchFunc(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
+	if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
+		return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "blpMatch", err)
+	}
+
+	level1 := args[0].(string)
+	level2 := args[1].(string)
+
+	return BlpMatch(level1, level2), nil
+}

cat <<'EOF' > blp_patch.txt
// BlpMatch determines whether level1 matches the level2 of BLP model.
func BlpMatch(level1 string, level2 string) bool {
	return level1 >= level2
}

// BlpMatchFunc is the wrapper for BlpMatch.
func BlpMatchFunc(args ...interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
	if err := validateVariadicArgs(2, args...); err != nil {
		return false, fmt.Errorf("%s: %w", "blpMatch", err)
	}

	level1 := args[0].(string)
	level2 := args[1].(string)

	return BlpMatch(level1, level2), nil
}
EOF
